const handleValidationErrors = (req, res, next) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
        // ĞÑ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ JSON Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ²ĞµÑ‚ Ñ Ğ´ĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ğ»ÑĞ¼Ğ¸ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±Ğ¾Ğº Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
        return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    }
    next();
};


const register = async (req, res, next) => {
    // Ğ’Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ° middleware Ğ² Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ğµ, handleValidationErrors Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ» Ğ±Ñ‹ 400
    const { username, password } = req.body;

    try {
        // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼, ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒĞµÑ‚ Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ Ñ Ñ‚Ğ°ĞºĞ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ĞµĞ¼
        const user = await User.findOne({ username: username.toLowerCase() }); // Ğ˜Ñ‰ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾ Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¶Ğ½ĞµĞ¼Ñƒ Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ñƒ
        if (user) {
            // 409 Conflict - Ñ€ĞµÑÑƒÑ€Ñ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒĞµÑ‚
            return res.status(409).json({ error: 'ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ Ñ Ñ‚Ğ°ĞºĞ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ĞµĞ¼ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒĞµÑ‚' });
        }

        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ (Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ Ğ±ÑƒĞ´ĞµÑ‚ Ğ·Ğ°Ñ…ÑÑˆĞ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½ middleware Ğ² Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ĞµĞ»Ğ¸)
        const newUser = new User({ username: username.toLowerCase(), password });
        await newUser.save();

        // ĞĞ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾ÑĞ»Ğµ Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
        req.session.user = { id: newUser._id, username: newUser.username };

        // 201 Created - ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾Ğµ ÑĞ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ñ€ĞµÑÑƒÑ€ÑĞ°
        res.status(201).json({ message: 'ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾ Ğ·Ğ°Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½', user: { id: newUser._id, username: newUser.username } });

    } catch (error) {
        // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºÑƒ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒÑˆĞµ Ğ² Ñ†ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ‡Ğ¸Ğº Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±Ğ¾Ğº
        next(error);
    }

const login = async (req, res, next) => {
    // Ğ’Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ°
    const { username, password } = req.body;

    try {
        // ĞĞ°Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾ Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ¸ (Ğ¸Ñ‰ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾ Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¶Ğ½ĞµĞ¼Ñƒ Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ñƒ)
        const user = await User.findOne({ username: username.toLowerCase() });
        if (!user) {
            // 401 Unauthorized - ĞĞµĞ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ ÑƒÑ‡ĞµÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ
            return res.status(401).json({ error: 'ĞĞµĞ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ¼Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ' });
        }

        // Ğ¡Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ²Ğ²ĞµĞ´ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ Ñ Ñ…ÑÑˆĞµĞ¼ Ğ¸Ğ· Ğ‘Ğ”
        const isMatch = await user.comparePassword(password);
        if (!isMatch) {
            // 401 Unauthorized - ĞĞµĞ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ ÑƒÑ‡ĞµÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ
            return res.status(401).json({ error: 'ĞĞµĞ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ¼Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ' });
        }

        // Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ ÑƒÑ‡ĞµÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ñ‹, Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ, ÑĞ¾Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½ÑÑ ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ğ² ÑĞµÑÑĞ¸Ğ¸
        req.session.user = { id: user._id, username: user.username };

        // 200 OK - ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´
        res.status(200).json({ message: 'ĞĞ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ°', user: { id: user._id, username: user.username } });

    } catch (error) {
        next(error);
    }
};

const getUsers = async (req, res, next) => {
    try {
        // ĞĞ°Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ²ÑĞµÑ… Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹, Ğ¸ÑĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ°Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğµ password

const ContactMessage = require('../models/contact');
const { validationResult } = require('express-validator');

// Ğ’ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ°Ñ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ¸ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±Ğ¾Ğº Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ (ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ ĞµÑÑ‚ÑŒ Ğ² auth, Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ÑˆĞµ Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚ÑŒ Ğ»Ğ¾ĞºĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾ Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ² Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ¼ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğµ)

const handleValidationErrors = (req, res, next) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
        return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    }
    next();
};

        const newMessage = new ContactMessage({ name, email, message });
        await newMessage.save();

        // 201 Created - ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾Ğµ ÑĞ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ñ€ĞµÑÑƒÑ€ÑĞ°
        res.status(201).json({ message: 'Ğ’Ğ°ÑˆĞµ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¾!' });

    } catch (error) {
        next(error); // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºÑƒ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒÑˆĞµ, Ğ²ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ°Ñ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Mongoose
    }

const getContactMessages = async (req, res, next) => {

=== backend\controllers\info.js ===
const os = require('os');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const path = require('path');

const getOSInfo = (req, res) => {
    const info = {
        platform: os.platform(),
        release: os.release(),
        uptime: os.uptime(),
        arch: os.arch()
    };
    res.status(200).json(info);
};

const getFileInfo = async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const filePath = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'data.txt');
        const data = await fs.readFile(filePath, 'utf8');
        res.status(200).json({ data });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(404).json({ error: 'Error reading file' });
    }
};

module.exports = {
    getOSInfo,
    getFileInfo
};

const handleValidationErrors = (req, res, next) => {
    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
        // ĞÑ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ JSON Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ²ĞµÑ‚ Ñ Ğ´ĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ğ»ÑĞ¼Ğ¸ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±Ğ¾Ğº Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

        res.status(200).json(products); // Content-Type: application/json ÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Express Ğ¿Ğ¾ ÑƒĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ‡Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ json()

    }

const getProductById = async (req, res, next) => {
    const { id } = req.params;
    try {
        // Mongoose Ğ±Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¸Ñ‚ CastError, ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ ID Ğ½ĞµĞ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ MongoID, Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ° Ğ±ÑƒĞ´ĞµÑ‚ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ¹Ğ¼Ğ°Ğ½Ğ° Ğ² catch
        const product = await Product.findById(id);
        if (!product) {
            const error = new Error('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½');
            error.status = 404;
            return next(error);
        }
        res.status(200).json(product);
    } catch (error) {
        // Ğ›Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ¼ CastError Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ´Ñ€ÑƒĞ³Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ¸ÑĞºĞ°
        if (error.kind === 'ObjectId' || error.name === 'CastError') {
            error.status = 400; // ĞĞµĞ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚ ID - ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ 400 Bad Request
            error.message = 'ĞĞµĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚ ID Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°';
        } else {
            error.status = 500; // Ğ”Ñ€ÑƒĞ³Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ - 500 Internal Server Error
            error.message = 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°';
        }
        next(error);
    }
};

const createProduct = async (req, res, next) => {
    // Ğ’Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ° middleware Ğ² Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ğµ, handleValidationErrors Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ» Ğ±Ñ‹ 400
    const { seller, name, description, price, category, quantity } = req.body;
    try {
        const newProduct = new Product({ seller, name, description, price, category, quantity });
        await newProduct.save();
        res.status(201).json(newProduct); // 201 Created
    } catch (error) {
        // Ğ›Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ ÑĞ¾Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ (Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€, Ğ¸Ğ·-Ğ·Ğ° Ğ¾Ğ³Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹ ÑÑ…ĞµĞ¼Ñ‹ Mongoose, ĞºÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğµ required, ĞºĞ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‹Ğµ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒÑÑ‚ÑÑ express-validator)
        next(error); // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºÑƒ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒÑˆĞµ
    }

const updateProduct = async (req, res, next) => {
    const { id } = req.params;
    // Ğ’Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ id Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ°
    const updates = req.body;
    // Ğ£Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ, ĞºĞ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶Ğ½Ñ‹ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ÑÑ‚ÑŒÑÑ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¼ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€ÑĞ¼ÑƒÑ
    delete updates._id;
    delete updates.createdAt;
    // updatedAt Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµÑ‚ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ÑÑ‚ÑŒÑÑ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸ Mongoose, ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ½Ğ°ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾ĞµĞ½Ñ‹ timestamps Ğ² ÑÑ…ĞµĞ¼Ğµ
    // Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ timestamps Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾ĞµĞ½Ñ‹, Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ğ·Ğ´ĞµÑÑŒ:
    updates.updatedAt = new Date();


    try {
        // { new: true } Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ²Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑƒĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚
        // { runValidators: true } Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿ÑƒÑĞºĞ°ĞµÑ‚ Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‹ Mongoose Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸ (Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹ Ñ validate)
        const updatedProduct = await Product.findByIdAndUpdate(id, updates, { new: true, runValidators: true });
        if (!updatedProduct) {
            const error = new Error('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ');
            error.status = 404;
            return next(error);
        }
        res.status(200).json(updatedProduct); // 200 OK
    } catch (error) {
        // Ğ›Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ (Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€, Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Mongoose, CastError)
        if (error.name === 'CastError' || error.kind === 'ObjectId') {
            error.status = 400;
            error.message = 'ĞĞµĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚ ID Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°';
        } else if (error.name === 'ValidationError') {
            // ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Mongoose Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ runValidators: true
            error.status = 400;
            // Mongoose ValidationError ÑĞ¾Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ¶Ğ¸Ñ‚ details, Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ñ€Ğ°ÑĞ¿Ğ°Ñ€ÑĞ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ, Ğ½Ğ¾ express-validator Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ÑˆĞµ
            error.message = `ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸: ${error.message}`; // Mongoose Validation Error message already contains details
        } else {
            error.status = 500;
            error.message = 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°';
        }
        next(error);
    }
};

const deleteProduct = async (req, res, next) => {
    const { id } = req.params;
    // Ğ’Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ id ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ°
    try {
        const deletedProduct = await Product.findByIdAndDelete(id);
        if (!deletedProduct) {
            const error = new Error('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ');
            error.status = 404;
            return next(error);
        }
        res.status(200).json({ message: 'ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½', deletedId: id }); // 200 OK
    } catch (error) {
        // Ğ›Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ¼ CastError Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ´Ñ€ÑƒĞ³Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸
        if (error.name === 'CastError' || error.kind === 'ObjectId') {
            error.status = 400;
            error.message = 'ĞĞµĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚ ID Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°';
        } else {
            error.status = 500;
            error.message = 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°';
        }
        next(error);
    }
};

const sortProducts = async (req, res, next) => {
    const { by, order = 'asc' } = req.query; // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€ÑĞ´Ğ¾Ğº (asc/desc)

    // Ğ‘Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ ÑĞ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸
    const allowedSortFields = ['category', 'seller', 'price', 'name', '_id', 'createdAt', 'updatedAt', 'quantity'];
    if (!allowedSortFields.includes(by)) {
        const error = new Error(`ĞĞµĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğµ ÑĞ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸. Ğ Ğ°Ğ·Ñ€ĞµÑˆĞµĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ: ${allowedSortFields.join(', ')}.`);
        error.status = 400;
        return next(error);
    }

    // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€ÑĞ´ĞºĞ° ÑĞ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸
    const sortOrder = (order.toLowerCase() === 'desc' || order === '-1') ? -1 : 1; // 1 for asc, -1 for desc

    try {
        const sortedProducts = await Product.find().sort({ [by]: sortOrder });
        res.status(200).json(sortedProducts);
    } catch (error) {
        next(error);
    }
};

module.exports = {
    getProducts,
    getProductById,
    createProduct,
    updateProduct,
    deleteProduct,
    sortProducts,
    handleValidationErrors // Ğ­ĞºÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ² Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ğ°Ñ… products
};

const authMiddleware = (req, res, next) => {
    // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼, ĞµÑÑ‚ÑŒ Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ğµ Ğ² ÑĞµÑÑĞ¸Ğ¸
    if (req.session && req.session.user) {
        // Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½, Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒÑˆĞµ
        next();
    } else {
        // Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½, Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚ÑƒÑ 401 Ğ¸ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ½Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñƒ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°
        // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ originUrl Ğ² query Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ° Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾ÑĞ»Ğµ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ° (Ğ¾Ğ¿Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾)
        res.status(401).redirect(`/auth?error=${encodeURIComponent('Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ')}&origin=${encodeURIComponent(req.originalUrl)}`);
    }
};

module.exports = authMiddleware;

const mongoose = require('mongoose');

const contactSchema = new mongoose.Schema({

    email: {
        type: String,
        required: true,
        trim: true,
        lowercase: true,

    },

const mongoose = require('mongoose');

const productSchema = new mongoose.Schema({
    seller: { type: String, required: true },
    name: { type: String, required: true },
    description: String,
    createdAt: { type: Date, default: Date.now },
    updatedAt: { type: Date, default: Date.now },
    price: { type: Number, required: true },
    category: String,
    quantity: Number
});

module.exports = mongoose.model('Product', productSchema);


=== backend\models\user.js ===
ï»¿// backend\models\user.js
const mongoose = require('mongoose');
const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs'); // Ğ”Ğ»Ñ Ñ…ÑÑˆĞ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹

const userSchema = new mongoose.Schema({
    username: { type: String, required: true, unique: true, trim: true, lowercase: true }, // Trim Ğ¸ lowercase Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ‹
    password: { type: String, required: true, minlength: 6 }, // ĞœĞ¸Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ´Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ
    createdAt: { type: Date, default: Date.now }
});

// Middleware Mongoose: Ñ…ÑÑˆĞ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´ ÑĞ¾Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ¸ĞµĞ¼
userSchema.pre('save', async function(next) {
    if (!this.isModified('password')) {
        return next();
    }
    try {
        const salt = await bcrypt.genSalt(10);
        this.password = await bcrypt.hash(this.password, salt);
        next();
    } catch (err) {
        next(err);
    }
});

// ĞœĞµÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ´ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑÑ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ²Ğ²ĞµĞ´ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ Ñ Ñ…ÑÑˆĞµĞ¼ Ğ² Ğ‘Ğ”
userSchema.methods.comparePassword = function(candidatePassword) {
    return bcrypt.compare(candidatePassword, this.password);
};


module.exports = mongoose.model('User', userSchema);

// Backend API URL (relative paths)
const API_URL = '/api/products';
const INFO_API_URL = '/api/info';
const AUTH_API_URL = '/api/auth';
const CONTACT_API_URL = '/api/contact';


// --- ĞĞ±Ñ‰Ğ¸Ğµ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ²ÑĞµÑ… ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ† ---

// ĞĞ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµÑ‚ ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚ÑƒÑ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ²ĞµÑ‚Ğ° Ğ² Ñ„ÑƒÑ‚ĞµÑ€Ğµ
const updateResponse = (res) => {
    const responseElement = document.getElementById('response-status');
    if (!responseElement) return;

    let text = "Ğ¡Ñ‚Ğ°Ñ‚ÑƒÑ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ²ĞµÑ‚Ğ°: ";
    let color = 'black';

    if (res instanceof Error) {
        text += `ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ‚Ğ¸ - ${res.message}`;
        color = 'red';
    } else if (res && typeof res.status === 'number') { // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼, Ñ‡Ñ‚Ğ¾ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑŠĞµĞºÑ‚ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ²ĞµÑ‚Ğ° fetch
        text += `${res.status} ${res.statusText}`;
        if (res.status >= 200 && res.status < 300) {
            color = 'green';
        } else if (res.status >= 400 && res.status < 500) {
            color = 'orange';
        } else if (res.status >= 500) {
            color = 'red';
        }
    } else if (typeof res === 'string') { // Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾ĞºĞ° (Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€, ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¾Ğ± Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞµ JS)
        text += res;
        color = 'red';
    } else {
        text += "ĞĞ¶Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ...";
    }

    responseElement.textContent = text;
    responseElement.style.color = color;
};


// Ğ˜Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ/Ñ€Ğ°ÑĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¾ĞºĞ¾Ğ² Ñ Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸ĞµĞ¹ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ»ĞºĞ¸
const initializeToggleForms = () => {
    let toggleFormContainers = document.querySelectorAll('.toggle-form_container');
    toggleFormContainers.forEach(container => {
        // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼, Ğ½Ğµ ÑĞ²Ğ»ÑĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ‡Ğ¸Ğº ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ²ÑĞ·Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¼
        if (container.dataset.listenerAttached) {
            return;
        }
        container.dataset.listenerAttached = 'true';

        container.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const section = container.closest('.func-section__vertical, .search_section, .filter_section, .sort_section'); // Ğ˜Ñ‰ĞµĞ¼ Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ¶Ğ°Ğ¹ÑˆĞ¸Ğ¹ Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒÑĞºĞ¸Ğ¹ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ´ĞµĞ»
            if (section) {
                const hiddenForm = section.querySelector('.hidden-form');
                const arrowIcon = container.querySelector('.arrow-down-icon');

                if (hiddenForm) {
                    const isVisible = hiddenForm.classList.contains('visible');
                    hiddenForm.classList.toggle('visible'); // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ñ‹

                    if (arrowIcon) {
                        // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ ĞºĞ»Ğ°ÑÑ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ»ĞºĞ¸ (Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ² CSS)
                        arrowIcon.classList.toggle('rotated', !isVisible);
                    }
                }
            }
        });

        // Ğ˜Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾Ğµ ÑĞ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ÑĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ»Ğ¾Ğº Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞµ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹
        const arrowIcon = container.querySelector('.arrow-down-icon');
        const isFormVisible = container.closest('section')?.querySelector('.hidden-form')?.classList.contains('visible');
        if (arrowIcon) {
            // Ğ£ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾Ğµ ÑĞ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ÑĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ»ĞºĞ¸ Ğ² Ğ·Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸ÑĞ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ñ‚ Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ñ‹
            arrowIcon.classList.toggle('rotated', isFormVisible);
            arrowIcon.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s ease'; // Ğ£Ğ±ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ğ¼ÑÑ, Ñ‡Ñ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµÑ…Ğ¾Ğ´ ÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½
        }
    });
};


// Helper function to display validation errors from server (from express-validator)
const displayErrors = (errors, errorsDivId) => {
    const errorsDiv = document.getElementById(errorsDivId);
    if (!errorsDiv) return;

    errorsDiv.innerHTML = ''; // Clear previous errors

    if (errors && Array.isArray(errors)) {
        let errorHtml = '<ul>';
        errors.forEach(err => {
            // err object from express-validator errors.array() has msg, param, etc.
            // Display just the message from the server validation
            errorHtml += `<li>${err.msg}</li>`;
        });
        errorHtml += '</ul>';
        errorsDiv.innerHTML = errorHtml;
    } else if (typeof errors === 'string') {
        errorsDiv.innerHTML = `<p>${errors}</p>`; // Display a single error string
    } else {
        // Fallback for unexpected error format
        errorsDiv.innerHTML = '<p>ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾ÑˆĞ»Ğ° Ğ½ĞµĞ¸Ğ·Ğ²ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ°.</p>';
    }
};

// Helper function to clear error/success messages
const clearMessages = (errorsDivId, successDivId) => {
    const errorsDiv = document.getElementById(errorsDivId);
    const successDiv = document.getElementById(successDivId);
    if(errorsDiv) errorsDiv.innerHTML = '';
    if(successDiv) successDiv.innerHTML = '';
};


// --- Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ“Ğ»Ğ°Ğ²Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹ (index.ejs) ---

// Fetch and display products on Main page
const fetchProducts = async () => {
    const productList = document.getElementById('product-list');
    if (!productList) return;

    productList.innerHTML = '<p>Ğ—Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ²...</p>';

    try {
        const response = await fetch(API_URL);
        if (!response.ok) {
            // Attempt to read JSON error response if available, otherwise just text
            const errorBody = await response.text(); // Read body as text first
            let errorDetail = errorBody;
            try {
                const jsonError = JSON.parse(errorBody);
                if (jsonError.error) errorDetail = jsonError.error;
            } catch (e) { /* body was not JSON */ }

            throw new Error(`ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° HTTP: ${response.status} ${response.statusText} - ${errorDetail}`);
        }
        const products = await response.json();
        updateResponse(response);
        renderProducts(products, 'product-list');

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching products:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        productList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: red;">ĞĞµ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¾ÑÑŒ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ñ‹.<br>${error.message || ''}</p>`;
    }
};

// Render products as cards
const renderProducts = (products, containerId) => {
    const productList = document.getElementById(containerId);
    if (!productList) return;

    productList.innerHTML = '';

    if (!Array.isArray(products)) {
        products = [products];
    }

    if (products.length === 0) {
        productList.innerHTML = '<p>ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ñ‹ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½Ñ‹.</p>';
        return;
    }


    products.forEach((product) => {
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'card';
        // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ data-id Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑƒĞ´Ğ¾Ğ±ÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ° Ğ¸Ğ´ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
        card.dataset.productId = product._id;

        card.innerHTML = `
            <div class="card_content">
                <h3>${product.name || 'Ğ‘ĞµĞ· Ğ½Ğ°Ğ·Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ'}</h3>
                <p><b>ĞšĞ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ³Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ:</b> ${product.category || 'ĞĞµ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¾'}</p>
                <p><b>Ğ¦ĞµĞ½Ğ°:</b> $${product.price != null ? product.price.toFixed(2) : 'ĞĞµ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¾'}</p> <!-- Ğ¤Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ñ†ĞµĞ½Ñƒ -->
                <p><b>ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°Ğ²ĞµÑ†:</b> ${product.seller || 'ĞĞµ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ğ½'}</p>
                <p><b>ĞšĞ¾Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¾:</b> ${product.quantity != null ? product.quantity : 'ĞĞµ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¾'}</p>
                <p><b>ĞĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ:</b> ${product.description || 'ĞĞµÑ‚ Ğ¾Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ'}</p>
           </div>
            <!-- ĞšĞ½Ğ¾Ğ¿ĞºĞ° ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ½Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğµ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ĞºĞ¸ -->
           ${containerId === 'admin-product-list' ? `<button class="button__delete" onclick="deleteProduct('${product._id}')"><img class="trash-icon" src="/icons/trash-2.svg" alt="Ğ£Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ"></button>` : ''}
        `;

        // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ ÑĞ¾Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğµ ĞºĞ»Ğ¸ĞºĞ° Ğ¢ĞĞ›Ğ¬ĞšĞ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ² Ğ½Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğµ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ĞºĞ¸
        if (containerId === 'admin-product-list') {
            card.classList.add('interactive');
            card.onclick = () => populateEditForm(product);
        }


        productList.appendChild(card);
    });
};

// Search for a product by ID on Main page
const searchProduct = async () => {
    const idInput = document.getElementById('search-id');
    const productList = document.getElementById('product-list');
    if (!idInput || !productList) return;

    const id = idInput.value.trim();

    if (!id) {
        alert('Ğ’Ğ²ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ ID Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ° Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ¸ÑĞºĞ°.');
        fetchProducts(); // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ¶Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ²ĞµÑÑŒ ÑĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ¾Ğº, ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğµ Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğµ
        return;
    }

    productList.innerHTML = '<p>ĞŸĞ¾Ğ¸ÑĞº...</p>';

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/${id}`);
        updateResponse(response);

        if (response.ok) {
            const product = await response.json();
            renderProducts([product], 'product-list');
        } else {
            const result = await response.headers.get('content-type')?.includes('application/json') ? await response.json() : { error: await response.text() };
            productList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: red;">${result.error || response.statusText || 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ¸ÑĞºĞµ'}</p>`;
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error searching product:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        productList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: red;">ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾ÑˆĞ»Ğ° Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ¸ÑĞºĞµ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°.</p>`;
    }
};

// Filter products by price range (Client-side filtering) on Main page
const filterProducts = async () => {
    const minPriceInput = document.getElementById('min-price');
    const maxPriceInput = document.getElementById('max-price');
    const productList = document.getElementById('product-list');
    if (!minPriceInput || !maxPriceInput || !productList) return;

    const minPrice = Number(minPriceInput.value) || 0;
    const maxPrice = Number(maxPriceInput.value) || Infinity;

    // Ğ¡Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ°Ğ»Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ’Ğ¡Ğ• Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ñ‹, Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ¼ Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ»ÑŒÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ½Ğ° ĞºĞ»Ğ¸ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğµ
    try {
        const response = await fetch(API_URL);
        if (!response.ok) {
            const errorBody = await response.text();
            let errorDetail = errorBody;
            try {
                const jsonError = JSON.parse(errorBody);
                if (jsonError.error) errorDetail = jsonError.error;
            } catch (e) { /* body was not JSON */ }
            throw new Error(`ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° HTTP: ${response.status} ${response.statusText} - ${errorDetail}`);
        }
        const products = await response.json();

        updateResponse(response);

        const filteredProducts = products.filter(
            (product) => product.price >= minPrice && product.price <= maxPrice
        );

        renderProducts(filteredProducts, 'product-list');

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error filtering products:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        productList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: red;">ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾ÑˆĞ»Ğ° Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ»ÑŒÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ².<br>${error.message || ''}</p>`;
    }
};


// Fetch and display OS information on Main page
const fetchOSInfo = async () => {
    const infoDisplay = document.getElementById('info-display');
    if (!infoDisplay) return;

    infoDisplay.innerHTML = '<p>Ğ—Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ° OS Info...</p>';

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${INFO_API_URL}/os`);
        if (!response.ok) {
            const errorBody = await response.text();
            let errorDetail = errorBody;
            try {
                const jsonError = JSON.parse(errorBody);
                if (jsonError.error) errorDetail = jsonError.error;
            } catch (e) { /* body was not JSON */ }
            throw new Error(`ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° HTTP: ${response.status} ${response.statusText} - ${errorDetail}`);
        }
        const osInfo = await response.json();

        updateResponse(response);
        displayInfo('Ğ˜Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¾Ğ± OS', osInfo, 'info-display');

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching OS info:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        displayInfo('Ğ˜Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¾Ğ± OS', { error: `ĞĞµ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¾ÑÑŒ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¾Ğ± OS.<br>${error.message || ''}` }, 'info-display');
    }
};

    }
};

// Display fetched information in a specific container
const displayInfo = (title, info, containerId) => {
    const infoDisplay = document.getElementById(containerId);
    if (!infoDisplay) return;

    let formattedInfo;
    if (typeof info === 'object') {
        formattedInfo = `<pre>${JSON.stringify(info, null, 2)}</pre>`;
    } else {
        formattedInfo = `<pre>${info}</pre>`; // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ ĞºĞ°Ğº Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑÑ‚
    }

    infoDisplay.innerHTML = `<h3>${title}</h3>${formattedInfo}`;
};

// Fetch and display sorted products (Server-side sorting) on Main page
const fetchSortedProducts = async (sortBy, order = 'asc') => { // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ° ÑĞ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€ÑĞ´ĞºÑƒ
    const productList = document.getElementById('product-list');
    if (!productList) return;

    productList.innerHTML = '<p>Ğ¡Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ°...</p>';

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/sort?by=${sortBy}&order=${order}`);
        if (!response.ok) {
            const result = await response.headers.get('content-type')?.includes('application/json') ? await response.json() : { error: await response.text() };
            throw new Error(result.error || `ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° HTTP: ${response.status} ${response.statusText}`);
        }
        const sortedProducts = await response.json();

        updateResponse(response);
        renderProducts(sortedProducts, 'product-list');

    } catch (error) {
        console.error(`Error sorting products by ${sortBy}:`, error);
        updateResponse(error);
        productList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: red;">${error.message || 'ĞĞµ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¾ÑÑŒ Ğ¾Ñ‚ÑĞ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ñ‹.'}</p>`;
    }
};


// --- Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹ ĞĞ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ĞºĞ¸ (admin.ejs) ---

// Fetch and display products on Admin page
const fetchAdminProducts = async () => {
    const productList = document.getElementById('admin-product-list');
    if (!productList) return;

    productList.innerHTML = '<p>Ğ—Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ² Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ĞºĞ¸...</p>';

    try {
        const response = await fetch(API_URL); // Ğ—Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ Ğ²ÑĞµÑ… Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ²
        if (!response.ok) {
            // Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ½Ğµ OK, Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ° Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ´Ñ€ÑƒĞ³Ğ°Ñ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ°
            const errorBody = await response.text();
            let errorDetail = errorBody;
            try {
                const jsonError = JSON.parse(errorBody);
                if (jsonError.error) errorDetail = jsonError.error;
            } catch (e) { /* body was not JSON */ }

            if (response.status === 401) {
                // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ½Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñƒ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚ authMiddleware Ğ½Ğ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğµ
                productList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: orange;">Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¼Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ².<br>${errorDetail || ''}</p>`;
            } else {
                productList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: red;">ĞĞµ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¾ÑÑŒ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ñ‹ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ.<br>${errorDetail || ''}</p>`;
            }
            throw new Error(`ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° HTTP: ${response.status} ${response.statusText} - ${errorDetail}`);
        }
        const products = await response.json();

        updateResponse(response);
        renderProducts(products, 'admin-product-list'); // Ğ ĞµĞ½Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ñ‹ Ğ² Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ĞºĞµ
        // ĞĞ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ĞºÑƒ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ²
        const totalProductsSpan = document.getElementById('total-products');
        if(totalProductsSpan) totalProductsSpan.textContent = products.length;


    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching admin products:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ²ĞµĞ´ĞµĞ½Ğ¾ Ğ² Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¾ĞºĞµ productList Ğ²Ñ‹ÑˆĞµ, Ğ·Ğ´ĞµÑÑŒ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ³Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼
    }
};

// Fetch and display contact messages on Admin page
const fetchContactMessages = async () => {
    const messagesList = document.getElementById('contact-messages-list'); // ID Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞºĞ° ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹
    if (!messagesList) return;

    messagesList.innerHTML = '<p>Ğ—Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ° ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹...</p>';

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${CONTACT_API_URL}/messages`); // API Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹
        if (!response.ok) {
            const errorBody = await response.text();
            let errorDetail = errorBody;
            try {
                const jsonError = JSON.parse(errorBody);
                if (jsonError.error) errorDetail = jsonError.error;
            } catch (e) { /* body was not JSON */ }

            if (response.status === 401) {
                messagesList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: orange;">Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¼Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ° ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹.<br>${errorDetail || ''}</p>`;
            } else {
                messagesList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: red;">ĞĞµ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¾ÑÑŒ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ.<br>${errorDetail || ''}</p>`;
            }
            throw new Error(`ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° HTTP: ${response.status} ${response.statusText} - ${errorDetail}`);
        }
        const messages = await response.json();

        updateResponse(response);

        messagesList.innerHTML = ''; // ĞÑ‡Ğ¸Ñ‰Ğ°ĞµĞ¼
        if (messages.length === 0) {
            messagesList.innerHTML = '<p>ĞĞµÑ‚ Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‹Ñ… ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹.</p>';
            return;
        }

        const messagesHtml = messages.map(msg => `
             <div class="message-item">
                 <p><b>ĞÑ‚:</b> ${msg.name} (${msg.email})</p>
                 <p><b>Ğ”Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ°:</b> ${new Date(msg.createdAt).toLocaleString()}</p>
                 <p>${msg.message}</p>
             </div>
         `).join('');
        messagesList.innerHTML = messagesHtml;

        // ĞĞ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ĞºÑƒ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹
        const totalMessagesSpan = document.getElementById('total-messages'); // Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½ ID
        if(totalMessagesSpan) totalMessagesSpan.textContent = messages.length;


    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching contact messages:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ²ĞµĞ´ĞµĞ½Ğ¾
    }
};

// Fetch and display users on Admin page
const fetchUsers = async () => {
    const usersList = document.getElementById('users-list-container'); // ID Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹
    if (!usersList) return;

    usersList.innerHTML = '<p>Ğ—Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹...</p>';

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${AUTH_API_URL}/users`); // API Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹
        if (!response.ok) {
            const errorBody = await response.text();
            let errorDetail = errorBody;
            try {
                const jsonError = JSON.parse(errorBody);
                if (jsonError.error) errorDetail = jsonError.error;
            } catch (e) { /* body was not JSON */ }

            if (response.status === 401) {
                usersList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: orange;">Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¼Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹.<br>${errorDetail || ''}</p>`;
            } else {
                usersList.innerHTML = `<p style="color: red;">ĞĞµ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¾ÑÑŒ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹.<br>${errorDetail || ''}</p>`;
            }
            throw new Error(`ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° HTTP: ${response.status} ${response.statusText} - ${errorDetail}`);
        }
        const users = await response.json();

        updateResponse(response);

        usersList.innerHTML = ''; // ĞÑ‡Ğ¸Ñ‰Ğ°ĞµĞ¼
        if (users.length === 0) {
            usersList.innerHTML = '<p>ĞĞµÑ‚ Ğ·Ğ°Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹.</p>';
            return;
        }

        const usersHtml = users.map(user => `
             <div class="user-item">
                 <p><b>Ğ˜Ğ¼Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ:</b> ${user.username}</p>
                 <p><b>ID:</b> ${user._id}</p>
                 <p><b>Ğ—Ğ°Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½:</b> ${new Date(user.createdAt).toLocaleString()}</p>
             </div>
         `).join('');
        usersList.innerHTML = usersHtml;

        // ĞĞ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ĞºÑƒ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹
        const totalUsersSpan = document.getElementById('total-users');
        if(totalUsersSpan) totalUsersSpan.textContent = users.length;

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching users:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ²ĞµĞ´ĞµĞ½Ğ¾
    }
};


// Populate the edit form with product data on Admin page
const populateEditForm = (product) => {
    const editForm = document.getElementById('edit-product-form');
    if (!editForm) return;

    editForm.querySelector('#edit-id').value = product._id;
    editForm.querySelector('#edit-name').value = product.name || '';
    editForm.querySelector('#edit-category').value = product.category || '';
    editForm.querySelector('#edit-description').value = product.description || '';
    editForm.querySelector('#edit-price').value = product.price != null ? product.price : '';
    editForm.querySelector('#edit-seller').value = product.seller || '';
    editForm.querySelector('#edit-quantity').value = product.quantity != null ? product.quantity : '';

    // ĞÑ‡Ğ¸Ñ‰Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¾Ğ± Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ°Ñ…/ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑ…Ğµ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ñ‹ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ
    clearMessages('edit-form-errors', 'edit-form-success');

    // ĞœĞ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸ Ñ€Ğ°ÑĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ñƒ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ ĞºĞ»Ğ¸ĞºĞµ
    const editFormSection = editForm.closest('.func-section__vertical'); // ĞĞ°Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒÑĞºÑƒÑ ÑĞµĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ
    if (editFormSection) {
        const hiddenForm = editFormSection.querySelector('.hidden-form');
        if (hiddenForm && !hiddenForm.classList.contains('visible')) {
            hiddenForm.classList.add('visible');
            // ĞĞ°Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµĞ¹Ğ½ĞµÑ€ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ»ĞºÑƒ
            const toggleContainer = editFormSection.querySelector('.toggle-form_container');
            const arrowIcon = toggleContainer?.querySelector('.arrow-down-icon');
            if (arrowIcon) {
                arrowIcon.classList.add('rotated'); // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ ĞºĞ»Ğ°ÑÑ rotated
            }
        }
    }
};

// Delete a product on Admin page
const deleteProduct = async (id) => {
    if (!confirm(`Ğ’Ñ‹ ÑƒĞ²ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ½Ñ‹, Ñ‡Ñ‚Ğ¾ Ñ…Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ Ñ ID ${id}?`)) {
        return;
    }

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/${id}`, {
            method: 'DELETE',
        });

        updateResponse(response);

        if (response.ok) {
            alert(`ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ Ñ ID ${id} ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½.`);
            fetchAdminProducts(); // ĞĞ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ ÑĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ¾Ğº
            // ĞÑ‡Ğ¸Ñ‰Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ñƒ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ, ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ² Ğ½ĞµĞ¹ Ğ±Ñ‹Ğ» ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚
            const editIdInput = document.getElementById('edit-id');
            if (editIdInput && editIdInput.value === id) {
                document.getElementById('edit-product-form').reset();
                clearMessages('edit-form-errors', 'edit-form-success');
            }

        } else {
            const result = await response.headers.get('content-type')?.includes('application/json') ? await response.json() : { error: await response.text() };
            console.error('Error deleting product:', result.error || response.statusText);
            alert(`ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°: ${result.error || response.statusText || 'ĞĞµĞ¸Ğ·Ğ²ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ°'}`);
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        alert(`ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾ÑˆĞ»Ğ° Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°.`);
    }
};

// Add a new product on Admin page
const handleAddProductSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    const addForm = document.getElementById('add-product-form');
    if (!addForm) return; // Check form existence
    const addErrorsDiv = document.getElementById('add-form-errors');
    const addSuccessDiv = document.getElementById('add-form-success');

    clearMessages('add-form-errors', 'add-form-success'); // Clear messages

    const product = {
        name: addForm.querySelector('#name').value.trim(),
        category: addForm.querySelector('#category').value.trim(),
        description: addForm.querySelector('#description').value.trim(),
        price: Number(addForm.querySelector('#price').value),
        seller: addForm.querySelector('#seller').value.trim(),
        quantity: Number(addForm.querySelector('#quantity').value),
    };

    // Simple client-side validation
    if (!product.name || !product.category || !product.seller || isNaN(product.price) || product.price <= 0 || isNaN(product.quantity) || product.quantity < 0) {
        displayErrors([{msg: 'ĞŸĞ¾Ğ¶Ğ°Ğ»ÑƒĞ¹ÑÑ‚Ğ°, Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ²ÑĞµ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ ĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ğ¾ (ĞĞ°Ğ·Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ, ĞšĞ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ³Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ, ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°Ğ²ĞµÑ†, Ğ¦ĞµĞ½Ğ°>0, ĞšĞ¾Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¾>=0).'}], 'add-form-errors');
        return;
    }


    try {
        const response = await fetch(API_URL, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            },
            body: JSON.stringify(product),
        });

        const result = await response.json();
        updateResponse(response);

        if (response.ok) {
            // alert('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½!'); // Removed alert
            addForm.reset();
            fetchAdminProducts(); // Refresh list
            if(addSuccessDiv) addSuccessDiv.innerHTML = '<p>ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½!</p>'; // Show success message
        } else {
            // Error handling based on status code and response body
            if (response.status === 400 && result.errors) {
                displayErrors(result.errors, 'add-form-errors');
            } else {
                displayErrors(result.error || response.statusText || 'ĞĞµĞ¸Ğ·Ğ²ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸.', 'add-form-errors');
                if (response.status === 401) {
                    window.location.href = `/auth?error=${encodeURIComponent('Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ')}`;
                }
            }
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error adding product:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        displayErrors('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾ÑˆĞ»Ğ° Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°.', 'add-form-errors');
    }
};

// Edit an existing product on Admin page
const handleEditProductSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const editForm = document.getElementById('edit-product-form');
    if (!editForm) return; // Check form existence
    const editErrorsDiv = document.getElementById('edit-form-errors');
    const editSuccessDiv = document.getElementById('edit-form-success');

    clearMessages('edit-form-errors', 'edit-form-success'); // Clear messages

    const id = editForm.querySelector('#edit-id').value.trim();
    if (!id) {
        displayErrors('ID Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ° Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ½Ğµ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ğ½.', 'edit-form-errors');
        return;
    }

    const updatedProduct = {};
    const name = editForm.querySelector('#edit-name').value.trim();
    const category = editForm.querySelector('#edit-category').value.trim();
    const description = editForm.querySelector('#edit-description').value.trim();
    const price = editForm.querySelector('#edit-price').value.trim();
    const seller = editForm.querySelector('#edit-seller').value.trim();
    const quantity = editForm.querySelector('#edit-quantity').value.trim();

    // Add fields only if they are not empty and pass basic client validation
    if (name !== '') updatedProduct.name = name;
    if (category !== '') updatedProduct.category = category;
    if (description !== '') updatedProduct.description = description;
    if (price !== '') {
        const numPrice = Number(price);
        if (!isNaN(numPrice) && numPrice > 0) updatedProduct.price = numPrice;
        else { displayErrors('Ğ¦ĞµĞ½Ğ° Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ° Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¼.', 'edit-form-errors'); return; }
    }
    if (seller !== '') updatedProduct.seller = seller;
    if (quantity !== '') {
        const numQuantity = Number(quantity);
        if (!isNaN(numQuantity) && numQuantity >= 0) updatedProduct.quantity = numQuantity;
        else { displayErrors('ĞšĞ¾Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¾ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ½ĞµĞ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¼.', 'edit-form-errors'); return; }
    }

    if (Object.keys(updatedProduct).length === 0) {
        displayErrors('ĞĞµÑ‚ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ.', 'edit-form-errors');
        return;
    }

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/${id}`, {
            method: 'PUT',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            },
            body: JSON.stringify(updatedProduct),
        });

        const result = await response.json(); // Expect JSON response
        updateResponse(response);

        if (response.ok) {
            // alert('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½!'); // Removed alert
            // editForm.reset(); // Keep data in form for potential further editing
            fetchAdminProducts(); // Refresh list
            if(editSuccessDiv) editSuccessDiv.innerHTML = '<p>ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½!</p>'; // Show success message
        } else {
            // Error handling
            if (response.status === 400 && result.errors) {
                displayErrors(result.errors, 'edit-form-errors');
            } else {
                displayErrors(result.error || response.statusText || 'ĞĞµĞ¸Ğ·Ğ²ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¸.', 'edit-form-errors');
                if (response.status === 401) {
                    window.location.href = `/auth?error=${encodeURIComponent('Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ')}`;
                } else if (response.status === 404) {
                    displayErrors('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ.', 'edit-form-errors');
                }
            }
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error editing product:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        displayErrors('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾ÑˆĞ»Ğ° Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°.', 'edit-form-errors');
    }
};


// --- Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹ ĞšĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ² (contact.ejs) ---

// ĞĞ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ° Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²ĞºĞ¸ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ñ‹
const handleContactFormSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    const contactForm = document.getElementById('contact-form');
    if (!contactForm) return; // Check form existence
    const contactErrorsDiv = document.getElementById('contact-form-errors');
    const contactSuccessDiv = document.getElementById('contact-form-success');
    if (!contactErrorsDiv || !contactSuccessDiv) return;

    clearMessages('contact-form-errors', 'contact-form-success'); // Clear messages

    const formData = new FormData(contactForm);
    const data = Object.fromEntries(formData.entries());

    // Simple client-side validation
    if (!data.name?.trim() || !data.email?.trim() || !data.message?.trim()) {
        displayErrors('ĞŸĞ¾Ğ¶Ğ°Ğ»ÑƒĞ¹ÑÑ‚Ğ°, Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ²ÑĞµ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ.', 'contact-form-errors');
        return;
    }


    try {
        const response = await fetch(CONTACT_API_URL, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            },
            body: JSON.stringify(data),
        });

        const result = await response.json(); // Expect JSON response
        updateResponse(response);

        if (response.ok) { // Status 200 or 201
            if(contactSuccessDiv) contactSuccessDiv.innerHTML = `<p>${result.message || 'Ğ’Ğ°ÑˆĞµ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¾!'}</p>`; // Show success message
            contactForm.reset(); // Clear form
            updateContactButtonState(); // Update button state
        } else {
            // Error handling
            if (response.status === 400 && result.errors) {
                displayErrors(result.errors, 'contact-form-errors');
            } else {
                displayErrors(result.error || response.statusText || 'ĞĞµĞ¸Ğ·Ğ²ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²ĞºĞµ.', 'contact-form-errors');
            }
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error sending message:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        displayErrors('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾ÑˆĞ»Ğ° Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²ĞºĞµ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ.', 'contact-form-errors');
    }
};

// Function to update the state of the contact form submit button
const updateContactButtonState = () => {
    const contactForm = document.getElementById('contact-form');
    const contactSubmitBtn = document.getElementById('contact-submit-btn');
    if (!contactForm || !contactSubmitBtn) return;

    const name = contactForm.querySelector('#contact-name')?.value;
    const email = contactForm.querySelector('#contact-email')?.value;
    const message = contactForm.querySelector('#contact-message')?.value;

    // Button is enabled only if all required fields are non-empty after trimming
    contactSubmitBtn.disabled = !(name?.trim() && email?.trim() && message?.trim());
};


// --- Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹ Auth (auth.ejs) ---

// Handling the login form submission
const handleLoginFormSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    const loginForm = document.getElementById('login-form');
    if (!loginForm) return; // Check form existence
    const loginErrorsDiv = document.getElementById('login-errors');
    const loginSuccessDiv = document.getElementById('login-success'); // Add this div in auth.ejs
    if (!loginErrorsDiv || !loginSuccessDiv) return;

    clearMessages('login-errors', 'login-success'); // Clear messages

    const username = loginForm.querySelector('#login-username').value.trim();
    const password = loginForm.querySelector('#login-password').value;

    if (!username || !password) {
        displayErrors('ĞŸĞ¾Ğ¶Ğ°Ğ»ÑƒĞ¹ÑÑ‚Ğ°, Ğ²Ğ²ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ¼Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ.', 'login-errors');
        return;
    }

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${AUTH_API_URL}/login`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({ username, password }),
        });

        const result = await response.json(); // Expect JSON response
        updateResponse(response);

        if (response.ok) { // Status 200 OK
            // alert('Ğ’Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ĞµĞ½ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾!'); // Removed alert
            if(loginSuccessDiv) loginSuccessDiv.innerHTML = '<p>Ğ’Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ĞµĞ½ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¾! ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ...</p>'; // Show success message

            // Redirect to the page user came from, or admin page by default
            const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            const originUrl = urlParams.get('origin') || '/admin';
            window.location.href = originUrl; // Perform redirect
        } else {
            // Error handling
            if (response.status === 400 && result.errors) {
                displayErrors(result.errors, 'login-errors');
            } else {
                displayErrors(result.error || response.statusText || 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğµ.', 'login-errors');
            }
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error logging in:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        displayErrors('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾ÑˆĞ»Ğ° Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğµ.', 'login-errors');
    }
};

// Handling the registration form submission
const handleRegisterFormSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    const registerForm = document.getElementById('register-form');
    if (!registerForm) return; // Check form existence
    const registerErrorsDiv = document.getElementById('register-errors');
    const registerSuccessDiv = document.getElementById('register-success'); // Add this div in auth.ejs
    if (!registerErrorsDiv || !registerSuccessDiv) return;

    clearMessages('register-errors', 'register-success'); // Clear messages

    const username = registerForm.querySelector('#register-username').value.trim();
    const password = registerForm.querySelector('#register-password').value;
    const password2 = registerForm.querySelector('#register-password2').value;

    if (!username || !password || !password2) {
        displayErrors('ĞŸĞ¾Ğ¶Ğ°Ğ»ÑƒĞ¹ÑÑ‚Ğ°, Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ²ÑĞµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ.', 'register-errors');
        return;
    }

    if (password !== password2) {
        displayErrors('ĞŸĞ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ½Ğµ ÑĞ¾Ğ²Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ´Ğ°ÑÑ‚!', 'register-errors');
        return;
    }

    // Simple client-side password length check (server validation is primary)
    if (password.length < 6) {
        displayErrors('ĞŸĞ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶ĞµĞ½ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼ÑƒĞ¼ 6 ÑĞ¸Ğ¼Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ².', 'register-errors');
        return;
    }


    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${AUTH_API_URL}/register`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({ username, password }),
        });

        const result = await response.json(); // Expect JSON response
        updateResponse(response);

        if (response.ok) { // Status 200 OK or 201 Created
            // alert('Ğ ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ°! Ğ¢ĞµĞ¿ĞµÑ€ÑŒ Ğ²Ñ‹ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ñ‹.'); // Removed alert
            if(registerSuccessDiv) registerSuccessDiv.innerHTML = '<p>Ğ ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ°! ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ...</p>'; // Show success message

            // Redirect to the page user came from, or admin page by default
            const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            const originUrl = urlParams.get('origin') || '/admin';
            window.location.href = originUrl; // Perform redirect
        } else {
            // Error handling
            if (response.status === 400 && result.errors) {
                displayErrors(result.errors, 'register-errors');
            } else {
                displayErrors(result.error || response.statusText || 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸.', 'register-errors');
                if (response.status === 409) { // Conflict - user already exists
                    displayErrors('ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ Ñ Ñ‚Ğ°ĞºĞ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ĞµĞ¼ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒĞµÑ‚.', 'register-errors');
                }
            }
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error registering:', error);
        updateResponse(error);
        displayErrors('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾ÑˆĞ»Ğ° Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸.', 'register-errors');
    }
};

// Initialize Auth page functionality (toggle forms, attach submit listeners)
const initializeAuthPage = () => {
    const loginFormContainer = document.getElementById('login-form-container');
    const registerFormContainer = document.getElementById('register-form-container');
    const showRegisterLink = document.getElementById('show-register-link');
    const showLoginLink = document.getElementById('show-login-link');
    const loginForm = document.getElementById('login-form');
    const registerForm = document.getElementById('register-form');
    const loginErrorsDiv = document.getElementById('login-errors');
    const registerErrorsDiv = document.getElementById('register-errors');

    // Only initialize if the key containers are found
    if (loginFormContainer && registerFormContainer && loginForm && registerForm) {

        // Toggle forms functionality
        showRegisterLink?.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            loginFormContainer.style.display = 'none';
            registerFormContainer.style.display = 'block';
            loginForm.reset();
            clearMessages('login-errors', 'login-success');
            registerForm.reset(); // Also reset register form when switching to it
            clearMessages('register-errors', 'register-success');
        });

        showLoginLink?.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            registerFormContainer.style.display = 'none';
            loginFormContainer.style.display = 'block';
            registerForm.reset(); // Also reset register form when switching from it
            clearMessages('register-errors', 'register-success');
            loginForm.reset();
            clearMessages('login-errors', 'login-success');
        });

        // Attach submit listeners to forms
        loginForm.addEventListener('submit', handleLoginFormSubmit);
        registerForm.addEventListener('submit', handleRegisterFormSubmit);

        // Check if there's an error message in the URL and display it
        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const errorMessage = urlParams.get('error');
        if (errorMessage) {
            // Decide which form's error div to use. Maybe display it above both forms.
            // For now, let's just display it in the login error div.
            if (loginErrorsDiv) {
                loginErrorsDiv.innerHTML = `<p>${decodeURIComponent(errorMessage)}</p>`;
                // Optional: Remove the error from the URL after displaying
                // urlParams.delete('error');
                // history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + '?' + urlParams.toString());
            }
        }
    }
};


// --- Ğ˜Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞµ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹ ---
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {

    // Initialize toggle/collapse functionality for form sections
    initializeToggleForms();

    // Check current page and initialize page-specific functionality
    if (document.getElementById('product-list')) {
        // This is the Main page (index.ejs)
        fetchProducts();
        // Attach event listeners for info and sort buttons (only present on main)
        document.getElementById('os-info-btn')?.addEventListener('click', fetchOSInfo);
        document.getElementById('file-info-btn')?.addEventListener('click', fetchFileInfo);
        document.getElementById('sort-by-category-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => { fetchSortedProducts('category'); });
        document.getElementById('sort-by-seller-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => { fetchSortedProducts('seller'); });
        document.getElementById('sort-by-price-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => { fetchSortedProducts('price'); });
        document.getElementById('sort-by-name-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => { fetchSortedProducts('name'); });
        document.getElementById('sort-by-quantity-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => { fetchSortedProducts('quantity'); });
        document.getElementById('sort-by-created-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => { fetchSortedProducts('createdAt', 'desc'); });
        document.getElementById('sort-by-updated-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => { fetchSortedProducts('updatedAt', 'desc'); });
    }

    if (document.getElementById('admin-product-list')) {
        // This is the Admin page (admin.ejs)
        fetchAdminProducts(); // Load product list for admin
        fetchContactMessages(); // Load messages
        fetchUsers(); // Load users

        // Attach submit listeners for add/edit forms (only present on admin)
        document.getElementById('add-product-form')?.addEventListener('submit', handleAddProductSubmit);
        document.getElementById('edit-product-form')?.addEventListener('submit', handleEditProductSubmit);
    }

    // Initialize Auth page functionality
    if (document.getElementById('login-form-container')) { // Check if the auth form container exists
        initializeAuthPage();
    }

    // Initialize Contact page functionality
    if (document.getElementById('contact-form')) { // Check if the contact form exists
        document.getElementById('contact-form')?.addEventListener('submit', handleContactFormSubmit);
        // Attach input listeners for button state update
        document.getElementById('contact-name')?.addEventListener('input', updateContactButtonState);
        document.getElementById('contact-email')?.addEventListener('input', updateContactButtonState);
        document.getElementById('contact-message')?.addEventListener('input', updateContactButtonState);
        updateContactButtonState(); // Initial button state check
    }

    // Attach click handler for the refresh button in the footer (globally)
    document.querySelector('footer .button__refresh')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
        // Determine which data to refresh based on the current page elements
        if (document.getElementById('product-list')) {
            fetchProducts(); // Refresh products on Main page
        } else if (document.getElementById('admin-product-list')) {
            fetchAdminProducts(); // Refresh products on Admin page
            fetchContactMessages(); // Refresh messages
            fetchUsers(); // Refresh users
        } else {
            // For other pages, this button might not be present or relevant
            alert('ĞĞ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ½ĞµĞ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ½Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğµ.');
        }
    });

});

const express = require('express');
const { register, login, getUsers, handleValidationErrors } = require('../controllers/auth'); // Ğ˜Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ handleValidationErrors Ğ¸ getUsers
const authMiddleware = require('../middlewares/auth'); // Ğ˜Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ authMiddleware
const { body } = require('express-validator');

const router = express.Router();

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
router.post('/register', [
    body('username').trim().notEmpty().withMessage('Ğ˜Ğ¼Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾'),
    body('password').isLength({ min: 6 }).withMessage('ĞŸĞ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶ĞµĞ½ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼ÑƒĞ¼ 6 ÑĞ¸Ğ¼Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ²')
], handleValidationErrors, register); // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ÑĞµĞ¼ handleValidationErrors

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
router.post('/login', [
    body('username').trim().notEmpty().withMessage('Ğ˜Ğ¼Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾'),
    body('password').notEmpty().withMessage('ĞŸĞ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ½')
], handleValidationErrors, login); // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ÑĞµĞ¼ handleValidationErrors

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ ÑĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹ (Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ĞµĞ½ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¼)
// Ğ’ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ authMiddleware Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµÑ‚ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ»ÑĞ±Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
// Ğ”Ğ»Ñ Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ĞºĞ¸ Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ° Ğ±Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞµ ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹ (is_admin Ğ¸ Ñ‚.Ğ¿.)
router.get('/users', authMiddleware, getUsers);


module.exports = router;

=== backend\routes\contact.js ===
ï»¿// backend\routes\contact.js
const express = require('express');
const { sendContactMessage, getContactMessages, handleValidationErrors } = require('../controllers/contact'); // Ğ˜Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ handleValidationErrors Ğ¸ getContactMessages
const authMiddleware = require('../middlewares/auth'); // Ğ˜Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ authMiddleware
const { body } = require('express-validator');

const router = express.Router();

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²ĞºĞ¸ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑĞ²ÑĞ·Ğ¸
router.post('/', [
    body('name').trim().notEmpty().withMessage('Ğ˜Ğ¼Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾'),
    body('email').isEmail().withMessage('ĞĞµĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚ email'),
    body('message').trim().notEmpty().withMessage('Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾')
], handleValidationErrors, sendContactMessage); // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ÑĞµĞ¼ handleValidationErrors

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑĞ²ÑĞ·Ğ¸ (Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ĞµĞ½ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¼)
router.get('/messages', authMiddleware, getContactMessages);


module.exports = router;

// backend\routes\index.js
const express = require('express');
const productRoutes = require('./products');
const infoRoutes = require('./info');
const authRoutes = require('./auth');
const contactRoutes = require('./contact'); // Ğ˜Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼

const router = express.Router();

// Ğ’Ğ°ÑˆĞ¸ ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒÑÑ‰Ğ¸Ğµ API Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ñ‹

// ĞĞ¾Ğ²Ñ‹Ğµ API Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ñ‹

=== backend\routes\products.js ===
// backend\routes\products.js
const express = require('express');
const {
    getProducts,
    getProductById,
    createProduct,
    updateProduct,
    deleteProduct,
    sortProducts,
    handleValidationErrors // Ğ˜Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼
} = require('../controllers/products');

const authMiddleware = require('../middlewares/auth'); // Ğ˜Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ authMiddleware
const { body, param, query } = require('express-validator'); // Ğ˜Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ body, param, query

const router = express.Router();

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑĞ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸ (Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ĞµĞ½ Ğ²ÑĞµĞ¼)
router.get('/sort', [
    query('by').optional().trim().notEmpty().withMessage('ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»Ğµ ÑĞ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµÑ‚ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚Ñ‹Ğ¼'),
    query('order').optional().trim().isIn(['asc', 'desc', '1', '-1']).withMessage('ĞĞµĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€ÑĞ´Ğ¾Ğº ÑĞ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸ (asc, desc, 1, -1)')
], handleValidationErrors, sortProducts);

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ²ÑĞµÑ… Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ² (Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ĞµĞ½ Ğ²ÑĞµĞ¼)
router.get('/', getProducts);

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ¾ ID (Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ĞµĞ½ Ğ²ÑĞµĞ¼)
router.get('/:id', [
    param('id').isMongoId().withMessage('ĞĞµĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ ID Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°')
], handleValidationErrors, getProductById);

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ñ‹ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ, Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ, ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿Ğ½Ñ‹ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¼
// Ğ’ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ authMiddleware Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµÑ‚ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ»ÑĞ±Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
// Ğ”Ğ»Ñ Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ĞºĞ¸ Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ° Ğ±Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞµ ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹ (is_admin Ğ¸ Ñ‚.Ğ¿.)

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑĞ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ° (Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ĞµĞ½ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¼)
router.post('/', authMiddleware, [
    body('name').trim().notEmpty().withMessage('ĞĞ°Ğ·Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ° Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾'),
    body('seller').trim().notEmpty().withMessage('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°Ğ²ĞµÑ† Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ½'),
    body('price').isFloat({ gt: 0 }).withMessage('Ğ¦ĞµĞ½Ğ° Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ° Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¼'),
    body('category').trim().notEmpty().withMessage('ĞšĞ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ³Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ°'),
    body('quantity').isInt({ gt: -1 }).withMessage('ĞšĞ¾Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¾ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ñ†ĞµĞ»Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ğ½ĞµĞ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¼')
], handleValidationErrors, createProduct);

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ° (Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ĞµĞ½ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¼)
router.put('/:id', authMiddleware, [
    param('id').isMongoId().withMessage('ĞĞµĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ ID Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°'),
    // Ğ”ĞµĞ»Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ Ğ¾Ğ¿Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¼Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸, Ñ‚.Ğº. Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµÑ‚ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ÑÑ‚ÑŒÑÑ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ²ÑĞµ
    body('name').optional().trim().notEmpty().withMessage('ĞĞ°Ğ·Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ° Ğ½Ğµ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµÑ‚ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚Ñ‹Ğ¼'),
    body('seller').optional().trim().notEmpty().withMessage('ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°Ğ²ĞµÑ† Ğ½Ğµ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµÑ‚ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚Ñ‹Ğ¼'),
    body('price').optional().isFloat({ gt: 0 }).withMessage('Ğ¦ĞµĞ½Ğ° Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ° Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¼'),
    body('category').optional().trim().notEmpty().withMessage('ĞšĞ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ³Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµÑ‚ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¹'),
    body('quantity').optional().isInt({ gt: -1 }).withMessage('ĞšĞ¾Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¾ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ñ†ĞµĞ»Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ğ½ĞµĞ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¼')
], handleValidationErrors, updateProduct);

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ° (Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ĞµĞ½ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¼)
router.delete('/:id', authMiddleware, [
    param('id').isMongoId().withMessage('ĞĞµĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ ID Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ°')
], handleValidationErrors, deleteProduct);


module.exports = router;

=== backend\server.js ===
// backend\server.js
const express = require('express');
const path = require('path');
const session = require('express-session');
const routes = require('./routes'); // API Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ñ‹
const connectDB = require('./middlewares/db');
const { logRequest, logError } = require('./utils/logger');

const server = express();

// Connect to MongoDB
connectDB();

// Middlewares - ĞŸÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ² Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾Ğ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€ÑĞ´ĞºĞµ
server.use(logRequest); // 1. Ğ’Ğ°Ñˆ middleware Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¾Ğ²

// 2. Ğ”Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€ÑĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³Ğ° Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ğ° Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ° (JSON Ğ¸ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ñ‹)
server.use(express.json());
server.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

// 3. ĞĞ°ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ¹ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑÑĞ¸Ğ¹ (Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†)
// Ğ’ĞĞ–ĞĞ: secret Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶ĞµĞ½ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ ÑƒĞ½Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ğ¸ Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒÑÑ Ğ² Ğ±ĞµĞ·Ğ¾Ğ¿Ğ°ÑĞ½Ğ¾Ğ¼ Ğ¼ĞµÑÑ‚Ğµ (Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€, Ğ² Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ¾ĞºÑ€ÑƒĞ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ)
server.use(session({
    secret: process.env.SESSION_SECRET || 'supersecretkeydefault', // Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ½ÑƒÑ Ğ¾ĞºÑ€ÑƒĞ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ´ĞµÑ„Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ‚
    resave: false,
    saveUninitialized: false, // ĞĞµ ÑĞ¾Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½ÑÑ‚ÑŒ ÑĞµÑÑĞ¸Ğ¸ Ğ±ĞµĞ· Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…
    cookie: { secure: false, maxAge: 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 } // secure: true Ğ´Ğ»Ñ HTTPS Ğ² Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°ĞºÑˆĞ½Ğµ, maxAge Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑÑ€Ğ¾ĞºĞ° Ğ¶Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ½Ğ¸
}));

// ĞĞ°ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ¹ĞºĞ° View Engine (EJS)
server.set('view engine', 'ejs');
server.set('views', path.join(__dirname, 'views'));

// Ğ˜Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ middleware Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾ÑĞ»Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ¹ĞºĞ¸ ÑĞµÑÑĞ¸Ğ¹
const authMiddleware = require('./middlewares/auth');


// --- 4. ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ñ‹ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ† ---
// Ğ ĞµĞ½Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ layout, Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°Ğ²Ğ°Ñ Ğ² Ğ½ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ pageTemplate Ğ¸ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ

// Ğ“Ğ»Ğ°Ğ²Ğ½Ğ°Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ° (ÑĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ¾Ğº Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ²)
server.get('/', (req, res) => {
    res.render('layout', {
        title: 'Ğ“Ğ»Ğ°Ğ²Ğ½Ğ°Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ°',
        user: req.session.user,
        pageTemplate: 'pages/index'
    });
});

// ĞŸĞ°Ğ½ĞµĞ»ÑŒ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ° (Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ¸Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¾ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸ĞµĞ¹)
server.get('/admin', authMiddleware, (req, res) => {
    res.render('layout', {
        title: 'ĞŸĞ°Ğ½ĞµĞ»ÑŒ ĞĞ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°',
        user: req.session.user,
        pageTemplate: 'pages/admin'
    });
});

// Ğ¡Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ° Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑĞ²ÑĞ·Ğ¸
server.get('/contact', (req, res) => {
    res.render('layout', {
        title: 'ĞĞ±Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ½Ğ°Ñ ÑĞ²ÑĞ·ÑŒ',
        user: req.session.user,
        pageTemplate: 'pages/contact'
    });
});

// Ğ¡Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ° Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¸ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°
server.get('/auth', (req, res) => {
    // Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½, Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ½Ğ° Ğ³Ğ»Ğ°Ğ²Ğ½ÑƒÑ Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ĞºÑƒ
    if (req.session.user) {
        return res.redirect('/admin'); // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ½Ğ° Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ĞºÑƒ, ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ²Ğ¾ÑˆĞµĞ»
    }
    res.render('layout', {
        title: 'Ğ’Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´ Ğ¸ Ğ ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ',
        user: null, // ĞĞ° ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ½ĞµÑ‚
        error: req.query.error, // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½ÑƒÑ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºÑƒ Ğ¸Ğ· URL (Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€, Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ· authMiddleware)
        pageTemplate: 'pages/auth'
    });
});

// ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ²Ñ‹Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ° (GET Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ‹)
server.get('/logout', (req, res) => {
    req.session.destroy(err => {
        if (err) {
            console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ²Ñ‹Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğµ:', err);
        }
        res.redirect('/auth'); // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ½Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñƒ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°
    });
});


// --- 5. ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ñ‹ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ API ---
server.use('/api', routes);


// --- 6. ĞĞ±ÑĞ»ÑƒĞ¶Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸Ñ… Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ² ---
// Ğ­Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ‚ middleware Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶ĞµĞ½ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ğ¾ÑĞ»Ğµ Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ² ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ† Ğ¸ API
server.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));


// --- 7. ĞĞ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ° 404 - Not Found ---
// Ğ­Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ‚ middleware Ğ±ÑƒĞ´ĞµÑ‚ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ·Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½, ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ½Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ½ Ğ¸Ğ· Ğ¿Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ñ‹Ğ´ÑƒÑ‰Ğ¸Ñ… Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ² (ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹, API, ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸ĞºĞ°) Ğ½Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¾ÑˆĞµĞ»
server.use((req, res, next) => {
    res.status(404).render('layout', { // Ğ ĞµĞ½Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¼Ğ°ĞºĞµÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ 404
        title: 'Ğ¡Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ° Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½Ğ°',
        user: req.session.user, // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ½Ğ° 404 Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğµ
        pageTemplate: 'pages/404'
    });
});

// --- 8. Middleware Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ¸ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±Ğ¾Ğº ---
server.use((err, req, res, next) => {
    logError(req, err); // Ğ›Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºÑƒ ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°
    console.error(err.stack); // Ğ’Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼ ÑÑ‚ĞµĞº Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ Ğ² ĞºĞ¾Ğ½ÑĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒ ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°

    // ĞĞ¿Ñ€ĞµĞ´ĞµĞ»ÑĞµĞ¼ ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚ÑƒÑ ĞºĞ¾Ğ´ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ (Ğ¿Ğ¾ ÑƒĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ‡Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ 500 Internal Server Error)
    const statusCode = err.status || 500;

    // ĞÑ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ JSON Ğ´Ğ»Ñ API Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¾Ğ² Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ HTML ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñƒ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‡Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¾Ğ²
    if (req.originalUrl.startsWith('/api/')) {
        res.status(statusCode).json({ error: err.message || 'Ğ’Ğ½ÑƒÑ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ½Ğ½ÑÑ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°' });
    } else {
        // Ğ ĞµĞ½Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñƒ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ Ñ Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¼Ğ°ĞºĞµÑ‚Ğ°
        // ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚ÑƒÑ Ğ¸ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ Ğ² ÑˆĞ°Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ½
        res.status(statusCode).render('layout', {
            title: `ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ${statusCode}`,
            user: req.session.user,
            pageTemplate: 'pages/error', // Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ½ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ° Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸
            errorStatus: statusCode,
            errorMessage: err.message || 'Ğ§Ñ‚Ğ¾-Ñ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾ÑˆĞ»Ğ¾ Ğ½Ğµ Ñ‚Ğ°Ğº! ĞŸĞ¾Ğ¶Ğ°Ğ»ÑƒĞ¹ÑÑ‚Ğ°, Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ±ÑƒĞ¹Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ¶Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ ÑĞ²ÑĞ¶Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµÑÑŒ Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ¶ĞºĞ¾Ğ¹.'
        });
    }
});


// Start server
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000; // Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ½ÑƒÑ Ğ¾ĞºÑ€ÑƒĞ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ´ĞµÑ„Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ‚
server.listen(PORT, () => {
    console.log(`Server is running on http://localhost:${PORT}`);
});

=== backend\utils\logger.js ===
// backend\utils\logger.js
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

// Ğ£Ğ±ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ğ¼ÑÑ, Ñ‡Ñ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ¿ĞºĞ° logs ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒĞµÑ‚
const logDir = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'logs');
if (!fs.existsSync(logDir)){
    fs.mkdirSync(logDir);
}
const logFilePath = path.join(logDir, 'requests.log');

// Middleware Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¾Ğ²
const logRequest = (req, res, next) => {
    const requestId = uuidv4();
    req.requestId = requestId; // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¸ÑĞ²Ğ°Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ ID Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑƒ

    const startTime = Date.now();
    res.on('finish', () => {
        const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
        const logEntry = `${new Date().toISOString()} | ID: ${requestId} | Method: ${req.method} | URL: ${req.originalUrl} | Status: ${res.statusCode} | Duration: ${duration}ms\n`;

        fs.appendFile(logFilePath, logEntry, (err) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Error writing log:', err);
            }
        });
    });

    res.on('error', (error) => {
        // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¸ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞµ Ğ² Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ†ĞµÑÑĞµ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ¸ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ°
        logError(req, error); // Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·ÑƒĞµĞ¼ logError Ñ req
    });

    next();
};

// Ğ›Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±Ğ¾Ğº (Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ·Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ÑÑ middleware Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ¸ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±Ğ¾Ğº Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€ÑĞ¼ÑƒÑ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ½ĞµĞ¾Ğ±Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¸)
const logError = (req, error) => {
    // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‡Ğ¸Ğµ req Ğ¸ requestId
    const requestId = req && req.requestId ? req.requestId : 'N/A';
    const method = req ? req.method : 'N/A';
    const url = req ? req.originalUrl : 'N/A';

    const errorEntry = `${new Date().toISOString()} | ID: ${requestId} | Method: ${method} | URL: ${url} | Error: ${error.message} | Stack: ${error.stack}\n`;
    const errorLogFilePath = path.join(logDir, 'errors.log'); // ĞÑ‚Ğ´ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±Ğ¾Ğº

    fs.appendFile(errorLogFilePath, errorEntry, (err) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error('Error writing error log:', err);
        }
    });
};

module.exports = { logRequest, logError };
